1///Module containing a contract's types and functions.
2/**
3
4```solidity
5library BN254 {
6    type BaseField is uint256;
7    type ScalarField is uint256;
8    struct G1Point { BaseField x; BaseField y; }
9}
10```*/

16    clippy::empty_structs_with_brackets
17)]

23    #[derive(Clone)]
24    pub struct BaseField(alloy::sol_types::private::primitives::aliases::U256);
25    const _: () = {
26        use alloy::sol_types as alloy_sol_types;
27        #[automatically_derived]
28        impl alloy_sol_types::private::SolTypeValue<BaseField>
29            for alloy::sol_types::private::primitives::aliases::U256
30        {
31            #[inline]
32            fn stv_to_tokens(
33                &self,
34            ) -> <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::Token<'_>
35            {
36                alloy_sol_types::private::SolTypeValue::<
37                    alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256>,
38                >::stv_to_tokens(self)
39            }
40            #[inline]
41            fn stv_eip712_data_word(&self) -> alloy_sol_types::Word {
42                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::tokenize(self)
43                    .0
44            }
45            #[inline]
46            fn stv_abi_encode_packed_to(&self, out: &mut alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8>) {
47                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<
48                    256,
49                > as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_encode_packed_to(self, out)
50            }
51            #[inline]
52            fn stv_abi_packed_encoded_size(&self) -> usize {
53                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<
54                    256,
55                > as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_encoded_size(self)
56            }
57        }
58        #[automatically_derived]
59        impl BaseField {
60            /// The Solidity type name.
61            pub const NAME: &'static str = stringify!(@ name);
62            /// Convert from the underlying value type.
63            #[inline]
64            pub const fn from(value: alloy::sol_types::private::primitives::aliases::U256) -> Self {
65                Self(value)
66            }
67            /// Return the underlying value.
68            #[inline]
69            pub const fn into(self) -> alloy::sol_types::private::primitives::aliases::U256 {
70                self.0
71            }
72            /// Return the single encoding of this value, delegating to the
73            /// underlying type.
74            #[inline]
75            pub fn abi_encode(&self) -> alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8> {
76                <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_encode(&self.0)
77            }
78            /// Return the packed encoding of this value, delegating to the
79            /// underlying type.
80            #[inline]
81            pub fn abi_encode_packed(&self) -> alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8> {
82                <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_encode_packed(&self.0)
83            }
84        }
85        #[automatically_derived]
86        impl alloy_sol_types::SolType for BaseField {
87            type RustType = alloy::sol_types::private::primitives::aliases::U256;
88            type Token<'a> =
89                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::Token<'a>;
90            const SOL_NAME: &'static str = Self::NAME;
91            const ENCODED_SIZE: Option<usize> =
92                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::ENCODED_SIZE;
93            const PACKED_ENCODED_SIZE: Option<usize> = <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<
94                256,
95            > as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::PACKED_ENCODED_SIZE;
96            #[inline]
97            fn valid_token(token: &Self::Token<'_>) -> bool {
98                Self::type_check(token).is_ok()
99            }
100            #[inline]
101            fn type_check(token: &Self::Token<'_>) -> alloy_sol_types::Result<()> {
102                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::type_check(
103                    token,
104                )
105            }
106            #[inline]
107            fn detokenize(token: Self::Token<'_>) -> Self::RustType {
108                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::detokenize(
109                    token,
110                )
111            }
112        }
113        #[automatically_derived]
114        impl alloy_sol_types::EventTopic for BaseField {
115            #[inline]
116            fn topic_preimage_length(rust: &Self::RustType) -> usize {
117                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<
118                    256,
119                > as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::topic_preimage_length(rust)
120            }
121            #[inline]
122            fn encode_topic_preimage(
123                rust: &Self::RustType,
124                out: &mut alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8>,
125            ) {
126                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<
127                    256,
128                > as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::encode_topic_preimage(rust, out)
129            }
130            #[inline]
131            fn encode_topic(rust: &Self::RustType) -> alloy_sol_types::abi::token::WordToken {
132                <alloy::sol_types::sol_data::Uint<256> as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::encode_topic(
133                    rust,
134                )
135            }
136        }

254    /**```solidity
255    struct G1Point { BaseField x; BaseField y; }
256    ```*/
257    #[allow(non_camel_case_types, non_snake_case, clippy::pub_underscore_fields)]
258    #[derive(Clone)]
259    pub struct G1Point {
260        #[allow(missing_docs)]
261        pub x: <BaseField as alloy::sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
262        #[allow(missing_docs)]
263        pub y: <BaseField as alloy::sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
264    }
265    #[allow(
266        non_camel_case_types,
267        non_snake_case,
268        clippy::pub_underscore_fields,
269        clippy::style
270    )]
271    const _: () = {
272        use alloy::sol_types as alloy_sol_types;
273        #[doc(hidden)]
274        type UnderlyingSolTuple<'a> = (BaseField, BaseField);
275        #[doc(hidden)]
276        type UnderlyingRustTuple<'a> = (
277            <BaseField as alloy::sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
278            <BaseField as alloy::sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
279        );
280        #[cfg(test)]
281        #[allow(dead_code, unreachable_patterns)]
282        fn _type_assertion(_t: alloy_sol_types::private::AssertTypeEq<UnderlyingRustTuple>) {
283            match _t {
284                alloy_sol_types::private::AssertTypeEq::<
285                    <UnderlyingSolTuple as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
286                >(_) => {},
287            }
288        }
289        #[automatically_derived]
290        #[doc(hidden)]
291        impl ::core::convert::From<G1Point> for UnderlyingRustTuple<'_> {
292            fn from(value: G1Point) -> Self {
293                (value.x, value.y)
294            }
295        }
296        #[automatically_derived]
297        #[doc(hidden)]
298        impl ::core::convert::From<UnderlyingRustTuple<'_>> for G1Point {
299            fn from(tuple: UnderlyingRustTuple<'_>) -> Self {
300                Self {
301                    x: tuple.0,
302                    y: tuple.1,
303                }
304            }
305        }
306        #[automatically_derived]
307        impl alloy_sol_types::SolValue for G1Point {
308            type SolType = Self;
309        }
310        #[automatically_derived]
311        impl alloy_sol_types::private::SolTypeValue<Self> for G1Point {
312            #[inline]
313            fn stv_to_tokens(&self) -> <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::Token<'_> {
314                (
315                    <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::tokenize(&self.x),
316                    <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::tokenize(&self.y),
317                )
318            }
319            #[inline]
320            fn stv_abi_encoded_size(&self) -> usize {
321                if let Some(size) = <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::ENCODED_SIZE {
322                    return size;
323                }
324                let tuple =
325                    <UnderlyingRustTuple<'_> as ::core::convert::From<Self>>::from(self.clone());
326                <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_encoded_size(&tuple)
327            }
328            #[inline]
329            fn stv_eip712_data_word(&self) -> alloy_sol_types::Word {
330                <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolStruct>::eip712_hash_struct(self)
331            }
332            #[inline]
333            fn stv_abi_encode_packed_to(&self, out: &mut alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8>) {
334                let tuple =
335                    <UnderlyingRustTuple<'_> as ::core::convert::From<Self>>::from(self.clone());
336                <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_encode_packed_to(
337                    &tuple, out,
338                )
339            }
340            #[inline]
341            fn stv_abi_packed_encoded_size(&self) -> usize {
342                if let Some(size) = <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::PACKED_ENCODED_SIZE {
343                    return size;
344                }
345                let tuple =
346                    <UnderlyingRustTuple<'_> as ::core::convert::From<Self>>::from(self.clone());
347                <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::abi_packed_encoded_size(
348                    &tuple,
349                )
350            }
351        }
352        #[automatically_derived]
353        impl alloy_sol_types::SolType for G1Point {
354            type RustType = Self;
355            type Token<'a> = <UnderlyingSolTuple<'a> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::Token<'a>;
356            const SOL_NAME: &'static str = <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolStruct>::NAME;
357            const ENCODED_SIZE: Option<usize> =
358                <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::ENCODED_SIZE;
359            const PACKED_ENCODED_SIZE: Option<usize> =
360                <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::PACKED_ENCODED_SIZE;
361            #[inline]
362            fn valid_token(token: &Self::Token<'_>) -> bool {
363                <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::valid_token(token)
364            }
365            #[inline]
366            fn detokenize(token: Self::Token<'_>) -> Self::RustType {
367                let tuple = <UnderlyingSolTuple<'_> as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::detokenize(token);
368                <Self as ::core::convert::From<UnderlyingRustTuple<'_>>>::from(tuple)
369            }
370        }
371        #[automatically_derived]
372        impl alloy_sol_types::SolStruct for G1Point {
373            const NAME: &'static str = "G1Point";
374            #[inline]
375            fn eip712_root_type() -> alloy_sol_types::private::Cow<'static, str> {
376                alloy_sol_types::private::Cow::Borrowed("G1Point(uint256 x,uint256 y)")
377            }
378            #[inline]
379            fn eip712_components(
380            ) -> alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<alloy_sol_types::private::Cow<'static, str>>
381            {
382                alloy_sol_types::private::Vec::new()
383            }
384            #[inline]
385            fn eip712_encode_type() -> alloy_sol_types::private::Cow<'static, str> {
386                <Self as alloy_sol_types::SolStruct>::eip712_root_type()
387            }
388            #[inline]
389            fn eip712_encode_data(&self) -> alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8> {
390                [
391                    <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::eip712_data_word(&self.x).0,
392                    <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::SolType>::eip712_data_word(&self.y).0,
393                ]
394                .concat()
395            }
396        }
397        #[automatically_derived]
398        impl alloy_sol_types::EventTopic for G1Point {
399            #[inline]
400            fn topic_preimage_length(rust: &Self::RustType) -> usize {
401                0usize
402                    + <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::topic_preimage_length(&rust.x)
403                    + <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::topic_preimage_length(&rust.y)
404            }
405            #[inline]
406            fn encode_topic_preimage(
407                rust: &Self::RustType,
408                out: &mut alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8>,
409            ) {
410                out.reserve(<Self as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::topic_preimage_length(rust));
411                <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::encode_topic_preimage(&rust.x, out);
412                <BaseField as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::encode_topic_preimage(&rust.y, out);
413            }
414            #[inline]
415            fn encode_topic(rust: &Self::RustType) -> alloy_sol_types::abi::token::WordToken {
416                let mut out = alloy_sol_types::private::Vec::new();
417                <Self as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::encode_topic_preimage(rust, &mut out);
418                alloy_sol_types::abi::token::WordToken(alloy_sol_types::private::keccak256(out))
419            }
420        }
421    };
422    use alloy::contract as alloy_contract;
423    /**Creates a new wrapper around an on-chain [`BN254`](self) contract instance.
424
425    See the [wrapper's documentation](`BN254Instance`) for more details.*/
426    #[inline]
427    pub const fn new<
428        T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
429        P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
430        N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
431    >(
432        address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address,
433        provider: P,
434    ) -> BN254Instance<T, P, N> {
435        BN254Instance::<T, P, N>::new(address, provider)
436    }
437    /**A [`BN254`](self) instance.
438
439    Contains type-safe methods for interacting with an on-chain instance of the
440    [`BN254`](self) contract located at a given `address`, using a given
441    provider `P`.
442
443    If the contract bytecode is available (see the [`sol!`](alloy_sol_types::sol!)
444    documentation on how to provide it), the `deploy` and `deploy_builder` methods can
445    be used to deploy a new instance of the contract.
446
447    See the [module-level documentation](self) for all the available methods.*/
448    #[derive(Clone)]
449    pub struct BN254Instance<T, P, N = alloy_contract::private::Ethereum> {
450        address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address,
451        provider: P,
452        _network_transport: ::core::marker::PhantomData<(N, T)>,
453    }
454    #[automatically_derived]
455    impl<T, P, N> ::core::fmt::Debug for BN254Instance<T, P, N> {
456        #[inline]
457        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
458            f.debug_tuple("BN254Instance").field(&self.address).finish()
459        }
460    }
461    /// Instantiation and getters/setters.
462    #[automatically_derived]
463    impl<
464            T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
465            P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
466            N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
467        > BN254Instance<T, P, N>
468    {
469        /**Creates a new wrapper around an on-chain [`BN254`](self) contract instance.
470
471        See the [wrapper's documentation](`BN254Instance`) for more details.*/
472        #[inline]
473        pub const fn new(address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address, provider: P) -> Self {
474            Self {
475                address,
476                provider,
477                _network_transport: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
478            }
479        }
480        /// Returns a reference to the address.
481        #[inline]
482        pub const fn address(&self) -> &alloy_sol_types::private::Address {
483            &self.address
484        }
485        /// Sets the address.
486        #[inline]
487        pub fn set_address(&mut self, address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address) {
488            self.address = address;
489        }
490        /// Sets the address and returns `self`.
491        pub fn at(mut self, address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address) -> Self {
492            self.set_address(address);
493            self
494        }
495        /// Returns a reference to the provider.
496        #[inline]
497        pub const fn provider(&self) -> &P {
498            &self.provider
499        }
500    }
501    impl<T, P: ::core::clone::Clone, N> BN254Instance<T, &P, N> {
502        /// Clones the provider and returns a new instance with the cloned provider.
503        #[inline]
504        pub fn with_cloned_provider(self) -> BN254Instance<T, P, N> {
505            BN254Instance {
506                address: self.address,
507                provider: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.provider),
508                _network_transport: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
509            }
510        }
511    }
512    /// Function calls.
513    #[automatically_derived]
514    impl<
515            T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
516            P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
517            N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
518        > BN254Instance<T, P, N>
519    {
520        /// Creates a new call builder using this contract instance's provider and address.
521        ///
522        /// Note that the call can be any function call, not just those defined in this
523        /// contract. Prefer using the other methods for building type-safe contract calls.
524        pub fn call_builder<C: alloy_sol_types::SolCall>(
525            &self,
526            call: &C,
527        ) -> alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder<T, &P, C, N> {
528            alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder::new_sol(&self.provider, &self.address, call)
529        }
530    }
531    /// Event filters.
532    #[automatically_derived]
533    impl<
534            T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
535            P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
536            N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
537        > BN254Instance<T, P, N>
538    {
539        /// Creates a new event filter using this contract instance's provider and address.
540        ///
541        /// Note that the type can be any event, not just those defined in this contract.
542        /// Prefer using the other methods for building type-safe event filters.
543        pub fn event_filter<E: alloy_sol_types::SolEvent>(
544            &self,
545        ) -> alloy_contract::Event<T, &P, E, N> {
546            alloy_contract::Event::new_sol(&self.provider, &self.address)
547        }
548    }
549}
550///Module containing a contract's types and functions.
551/**
552
553```solidity
554library IPlonkVerifier {
555    struct PlonkProof { BN254.G1Point wire0; BN254.G1Point wire1; BN254.G1Point wire2; BN254.G1Point wire3; BN254.G1Point wire4; BN254.G1Point prodPerm; BN254.G1Point split0; BN254.G1Point split1; BN254.G1Point split2; BN254.G1Point split3; BN254.G1Point split4; BN254.G1Point zeta; BN254.G1Point zetaOmega; BN254.ScalarField wireEval0; BN254.ScalarField wireEval1; BN254.ScalarField wireEval2; BN254.ScalarField wireEval3; BN254.ScalarField wireEval4; BN254.ScalarField sigmaEval0; BN254.ScalarField sigmaEval1; BN254.ScalarField sigmaEval2; BN254.ScalarField sigmaEval3; BN254.ScalarField prodPermZetaOmegaEval; }

1132            #[inline]
1133            fn encode_topic(rust: &Self::RustType) -> alloy_sol_types::abi::token::WordToken {
1134                let mut out = alloy_sol_types::private::Vec::new();
1135                <Self as alloy_sol_types::EventTopic>::encode_topic_preimage(rust, &mut out);
1136                alloy_sol_types::abi::token::WordToken(alloy_sol_types::private::keccak256(out))
1137            }
1138        }

3266            };
3267            DECODE_SHIMS[idx](data, validate)
3268        }
3269        #[inline]
3270        fn abi_encoded_size(&self) -> usize {
3271            match self {
3272                Self::UnsupportedDegree(inner) => {
3273                    <UnsupportedDegree as alloy_sol_types::SolError>::abi_encoded_size(inner)
3274                },
3275            }
3276        }
3277        #[inline]
3278        fn abi_encode_raw(&self, out: &mut alloy_sol_types::private::Vec<u8>) {
3279            match self {
3280                Self::UnsupportedDegree(inner) => {
3281                    <UnsupportedDegree as alloy_sol_types::SolError>::abi_encode_raw(inner, out)
3282                },
3283            }
3284        }
3285    }

3317    /**Creates a `RawCallBuilder` for deploying this contract using the given `provider`
3318    and constructor arguments, if any.

3320    This is a simple wrapper around creating a `RawCallBuilder` with the data set to
3321    the bytecode concatenated with the constructor's ABI-encoded arguments.*/
3322    #[inline]
3323    pub fn deploy_builder<
3324        T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
3325        P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
3326        N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
3327    >(

3331    }
3332    /**A [`PlonkVerifier2`](self) instance.
3333
3334    Contains type-safe methods for interacting with an on-chain instance of the
3335    [`PlonkVerifier2`](self) contract located at a given `address`, using a given
3336    provider `P`.
3337
3338    If the contract bytecode is available (see the [`sol!`](alloy_sol_types::sol!)
3339    documentation on how to provide it), the `deploy` and `deploy_builder` methods can
3340    be used to deploy a new instance of the contract.
3341
3342    See the [module-level documentation](self) for all the available methods.*/
3343    #[derive(Clone)]
3344    pub struct PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N = alloy_contract::private::Ethereum> {
3345        address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address,
3346        provider: P,
3347        _network_transport: ::core::marker::PhantomData<(N, T)>,
3348    }
3349    #[automatically_derived]
3350    impl<T, P, N> ::core::fmt::Debug for PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N> {
3351        #[inline]
3352        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
3353            f.debug_tuple("PlonkVerifier2Instance")
3354                .field(&self.address)
3355                .finish()
3356        }
3357    }
3358    /// Instantiation and getters/setters.
3359    #[automatically_derived]
3360    impl<
3361            T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
3362            P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
3363            N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
3364        > PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N>
3365    {
3366        /**Creates a new wrapper around an on-chain [`PlonkVerifier2`](self) contract instance.
3367
3368        See the [wrapper's documentation](`PlonkVerifier2Instance`) for more details.*/
3369        #[inline]
3370        pub const fn new(address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address, provider: P) -> Self {
3371            Self {
3372                address,
3373                provider,
3374                _network_transport: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
3375            }
3376        }
3377        /**Deploys this contract using the given `provider` and constructor arguments, if any.
3378
3379        Returns a new instance of the contract, if the deployment was successful.
3380
3381        For more fine-grained control over the deployment process, use [`deploy_builder`] instead.*/
3382        #[inline]
3383        pub async fn deploy(
3384            provider: P,
3385        ) -> alloy_contract::Result<PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N>> {
3386            let call_builder = Self::deploy_builder(provider);
3387            let contract_address = call_builder.deploy().await?;
3388            Ok(Self::new(contract_address, call_builder.provider))
3389        }
3390        /**Creates a `RawCallBuilder` for deploying this contract using the given `provider`
3391        and constructor arguments, if any.
3392
3393        This is a simple wrapper around creating a `RawCallBuilder` with the data set to
3394        the bytecode concatenated with the constructor's ABI-encoded arguments.*/
3395        #[inline]
3396        pub fn deploy_builder(provider: P) -> alloy_contract::RawCallBuilder<T, P, N> {
3397            alloy_contract::RawCallBuilder::new_raw_deploy(
3398                provider,
3399                ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&BYTECODE),
3400            )
3401        }
3402        /// Returns a reference to the address.
3403        #[inline]
3404        pub const fn address(&self) -> &alloy_sol_types::private::Address {
3405            &self.address
3406        }
3407        /// Sets the address.
3408        #[inline]
3409        pub fn set_address(&mut self, address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address) {
3410            self.address = address;
3411        }
3412        /// Sets the address and returns `self`.
3413        pub fn at(mut self, address: alloy_sol_types::private::Address) -> Self {
3414            self.set_address(address);
3415            self
3416        }
3417        /// Returns a reference to the provider.
3418        #[inline]
3419        pub const fn provider(&self) -> &P {
3420            &self.provider
3421        }
3422    }
3423    impl<T, P: ::core::clone::Clone, N> PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, &P, N> {
3424        /// Clones the provider and returns a new instance with the cloned provider.
3425        #[inline]
3426        pub fn with_cloned_provider(self) -> PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N> {
3427            PlonkVerifier2Instance {
3428                address: self.address,
3429                provider: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.provider),
3430                _network_transport: ::core::marker::PhantomData,
3431            }
3432        }
3433    }
3434    /// Function calls.
3435    #[automatically_derived]
3436    impl<
3437            T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
3438            P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
3439            N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
3440        > PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N>
3441    {
3442        /// Creates a new call builder using this contract instance's provider and address.
3443        ///
3444        /// Note that the call can be any function call, not just those defined in this
3445        /// contract. Prefer using the other methods for building type-safe contract calls.
3446        pub fn call_builder<C: alloy_sol_types::SolCall>(
3447            &self,
3448            call: &C,
3449        ) -> alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder<T, &P, C, N> {
3450            alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder::new_sol(&self.provider, &self.address, call)
3451        }
3452        ///Creates a new call builder for the [`P_MOD`] function.
3453        pub fn P_MOD(&self) -> alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder<T, &P, P_MODCall, N> {
3454            self.call_builder(&P_MODCall {})
3455        }
3456        ///Creates a new call builder for the [`R_MOD`] function.
3457        pub fn R_MOD(&self) -> alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder<T, &P, R_MODCall, N> {
3458            self.call_builder(&R_MODCall {})
3459        }
3460        ///Creates a new call builder for the [`verify`] function.
3461        pub fn verify(
3462            &self,
3463            vk: <IPlonkVerifier::VerifyingKey as alloy::sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
3464            publicInput: [alloy::sol_types::private::primitives::aliases::U256; 7usize],
3465            proof: <IPlonkVerifier::PlonkProof as alloy::sol_types::SolType>::RustType,
3466        ) -> alloy_contract::SolCallBuilder<T, &P, verifyCall, N> {
3467            self.call_builder(&verifyCall {
3468                vk,
3469                publicInput,
3470                proof,
3471            })
3472        }
3473    }

3475    #[automatically_derived]
3476    impl<
3477            T: alloy_contract::private::Transport + ::core::clone::Clone,
3478            P: alloy_contract::private::Provider<T, N>,
3479            N: alloy_contract::private::Network,
3480        > PlonkVerifier2Instance<T, P, N>
3481    {
3482        /// Creates a new event filter using this contract instance's provider and address.
3483        ///
3484        /// Note that the type can be any event, not just those defined in this contract.
3485        /// Prefer using the other methods for building type-safe event filters.
3486        pub fn event_filter<E: alloy_sol_types::SolEvent>(
3487            &self,
3488        ) -> alloy_contract::Event<T, &P, E, N> {
3489            alloy_contract::Event::new_sol(&self.provider, &self.address)
3490        }
